The specified framework must be installed.\n    \n    If no framework is specified, will default to the one currently installed. If no framework is specified and both frameworks are installed, will default to the framework of the `model`, or to PyTorch if no model is provided.\n    \n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.task)**task** (`str`, defaults to `\"\"`) ‚Äî A task-identifier for the pipeline.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.num_workers)**num\\_workers** (`int`, _optional_, defaults to 8) ‚Äî When the pipeline will use _DataLoader_ (when passing a dataset, on GPU for a Pytorch model), the number of workers to be used.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.batch_size)**batch\\_size** (`int`, _optional_, defaults to 1) ‚Äî When the pipeline will use _DataLoader_ (when passing a dataset, on GPU for a Pytorch model), the size of the batch to use, for inference this is not always beneficial, please read [Batching with pipelines](https://huggingface.co/transformers/main_classes/pipelines.html#pipeline-batching) .\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.args_parser)**args\\_parser** ([ArgumentHandler](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/v4.48.1/en/internal/pipelines_utils#transformers.pipelines.ArgumentHandler), _optional_) ‚Äî Reference to the object in charge of parsing supplied pipeline parameters.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.device)**device** (`int`, _optional_, defaults to -1) ‚Äî Device ordinal for CPU/GPU supports. Setting this to -1 will leverage CPU, a positive will run the model on the associated CUDA device id. You can pass native `torch.device` or a `str` too\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.torch_dtype)**torch\\_dtype** (`str` or `torch.dtype`, _optional_) ‚Äî Sent directly as `model_kwargs` (just a simpler shortcut) to use the available precision for this model (`torch.float16`, `torch.bfloat16`, ‚Ä¶ or `\"auto\"`)\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.binary_output)**binary\\_output** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) ‚Äî Flag indicating if the output the pipeline should happen in a serialized format (i.e., pickle) or as the raw output data e.g. text.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.points_per_batch)**points\\_per\\_batch** (_optional_, int, default to 64) ‚Äî Sets the number of points run simultaneously by the model. Higher numbers may be faster but use more GPU memory.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.output_bboxes_mask)**output\\_bboxes\\_mask** (`bool`, _optional_, default to `False`) ‚Äî Whether or not to output the bounding box predictions.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.output_rle_masks)**output\\_rle\\_masks** (`bool`, _optional_, default to `False`) ‚Äî Whether or not to output the masks in `RLE` format\n\nAutomatic mask generation for images using `SamForMaskGeneration`. This pipeline predicts binary masks for an image, given an image. It is a `ChunkPipeline` because you can seperate the points in a mini-batch in order to avoid OOM issues. Use the `points_per_batch` argument to control the number of points that will be processed at the same time. Default is `64`.\n\nThe pipeline works in 3 steps:\n\n1.  `preprocess`: A grid of 1024 points evenly separated is generated along with bounding boxes and point labels. For more details on how the points and bounding boxes are created, check the `_generate_crop_boxes` function. The image is also preprocessed using the `image_processor`. This function `yields` a minibatch of `points_per_batch`.\n    \n2.  `forward`: feeds the outputs of `preprocess` to the model. The image embedding is computed only once. Calls both `self.model.get_image_embeddings` and makes sure that the gradients are not computed, and the tensors and models are on the same device.\n    \n3.  `postprocess`: The most important part of the automatic mask generation happens here. Three steps are induced:\n    \n    *   image\\_processor.postprocess\\_masks (run on each minibatch loop): takes in the raw output masks, resizes them according to the image size, and transforms there to binary masks.\n    *   image\\_processor.filter\\_masks (on each minibatch loop): uses both `pred_iou_thresh` and `stability_scores`. Also applies a variety of filters based on non maximum suppression to remove bad masks.\n    *   image\\_processor.postprocess\\_masks\\_for\\_amg applies the NSM on the mask to only keep relevant ones.\n\n[](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.example)Example:\n\nCopied\n\n\\>\\>\\> from transformers import pipeline\n\n\\>\\>\\> generator = pipeline(model=\"facebook/sam-vit-base\", task=\"mask-generation\")\n\\>\\>\\> outputs = generator(\n...     \"http://images.cocodataset.org/val2017/000000039769.jpg\",\n... )\n\n\\>\\>\\> outputs = generator(\n...     \"https://huggingface.co/datasets/Narsil/image\\_dummy/raw/main/parrots.png\", points\\_per\\_batch=128\n... )\n\nLearn more about the basics of using a pipeline in the [pipeline tutorial](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/pipeline_tutorial)\n\nThis segmentation pipeline can currently be loaded from [pipeline()](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/v4.48.1/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.pipeline) using the following task identifier: `\"mask-generation\"`.\n\nSee the list of available models on [huggingface.co/models](https://huggingface.co/models?filter=mask-generation).\n\n#### \\_\\_call\\_\\_\n\n[](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__)[< source \\>](https://github.com/huggingface/transformers/blob/v4.48.1/src/transformers/pipelines/mask_generation.py#L128)( image\\*argsnum\\_workers = Nonebatch\\_size = None\\*\\*kwargs ) ‚Üí `Dict`\n\nExpand 10 parameters\n\nParameters\n\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.inputs)**inputs** (`np.ndarray` or `bytes` or `str` or `dict`) ‚Äî Image or list of images.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.mask_threshold)**mask\\_threshold** (`float`, _optional_, defaults to 0.0) ‚Äî Threshold to use when turning the predicted masks into binary values.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.pred_iou_thresh)**pred\\_iou\\_thresh** (`float`, _optional_, defaults to 0.88) ‚Äî A filtering threshold in `[0,1]` applied on the model‚Äôs predicted mask quality.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.stability_score_thresh)**stability\\_score\\_thresh** (`float`, _optional_, defaults to 0.95) ‚Äî A filtering threshold in `[0,1]`, using the stability of the mask under changes to the cutoff used to binarize the model‚Äôs mask predictions.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.stability_score_offset)**stability\\_score\\_offset** (`int`, _optional_, defaults to 1) ‚Äî The amount to shift the cutoff when calculated the stability score.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.crops_nms_thresh)**crops\\_nms\\_thresh** (`float`, _optional_, defaults to 0.7) ‚Äî The box IoU cutoff used by non-maximal suppression to filter duplicate masks.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.crops_n_layers)**crops\\_n\\_layers** (`int`, _optional_, defaults to 0) ‚Äî If `crops_n_layers>0`, mask prediction will be run again on crops of the image. Sets the number of layers to run, where each layer has 2\\*\\*i\\_layer number of image crops.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.crop_overlap_ratio)**crop\\_overlap\\_ratio** (`float`, _optional_, defaults to `512 / 1500`) ‚Äî Sets the degree to which crops overlap. In the first crop layer, crops will overlap by this fraction of the image length. Later layers with more crops scale down this overlap.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.crop_n_points_downscale_factor)**crop\\_n\\_points\\_downscale\\_factor** (`int`, _optional_, defaults to `1`) ‚Äî The number of points-per-side sampled in layer n is scaled down by crop\\_n\\_points\\_downscale\\_factor\\*\\*n.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.MaskGenerationPipeline.__call__.timeout)**timeout** (`float`, _optional_, defaults to None) ‚Äî The maximum time in seconds to wait for fetching images from the web. If None, no timeout is set and the call may block forever.\n\nReturns\n\n`Dict`\n\nA dictionary with the following keys:\n\n*   **mask** (`PIL.Image`) ‚Äî A binary mask of the detected object as a PIL Image of shape `(width, height)` of the original image. Returns a mask filled with zeros if no object is found.\n*   **score** (_optional_ `float`) ‚Äî Optionally, when the model is capable of estimating a confidence of the ‚Äúobject‚Äù described by the label and the mask.\n\nGenerates binary segmentation masks\n\n### [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.VisualQuestionAnsweringPipeline)VisualQuestionAnsweringPipeline\n\n### class transformers.VisualQuestionAnsweringPipeline\n\n[](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.VisualQuestionAnsweringPipeline)[< source \\>](https://github.com/huggingface/transformers/blob/v4.48.1/src/transformers/pipelines/visual_question_answering.py#L19)( \\*args\\*\\*kwargs )\n\nExpand 12 parameters\n\nParameters\n\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.VisualQuestionAnsweringPipeline.model)**model** ([PreTrainedModel](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/v4.48.1/en/main_classes/model#transformers.PreTrainedModel) or [TFPreTrainedModel](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/v4.48.1/en/main_classes/model#transformers.TFPreTrainedModel)) ‚Äî The model that will be used by the pipeline to make predictions. The specified framework must be installed.\n    \n    If no framework is specified, will default to the one currently installed. This pipeline is currently only available in PyTorch.\n\n[](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.VisualQuestionAnsweringPipeline.example)Example:\n\nCopied\n\n\\>\\>\\> from transformers import pipeline\n\n\\>\\>\\> oracle = pipeline(model=\"dandelin/vilt-b32-finetuned-vqa\")\n\\>\\>\\> image\\_url = \"https://huggingface.co/datasets/Narsil/image\\_dummy/raw/main/lena.png\"\n\\>\\>\\> oracle(question=\"What is she wearing ?\", image=image\\_url)\n\\[{'score': 0.948, 'answer': 'hat'}, {'score': 0.009, 'answer': 'fedora'}, {'score': 0.003, 'answer': 'clothes'}, {'score': 0.003, 'answer': 'sun hat'}, {'score': 0.002, 'answer': 'nothing'}\\]\n\n\\>\\>\\> oracle(question=\"What is she wearing ?\", image=image\\_url, top\\_k=1)\n\\[{'score': 0.948, 'answer': 'hat'}\\]\n\n\\>\\>\\> oracle(question=\"Is this a person ?\", image=image\\_url, top\\_k=1)\n\\[{'score': 0.993, 'answer': 'yes'}\\]\n\n\\>\\>\\> oracle(question=\"Is this a man ?\", image=image\\_url, top\\_k=1)\n\\[{'score': 0.996, 'answer': 'no'}\\]\n\nLearn more about the basics of using a pipeline in the [pipeline tutorial](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/pipeline_tutorial)\n\nThis visual question answering pipeline can currently be loaded from [pipeline()](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/v4.48.1/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.pipeline) using the following task identifiers: `\"visual-question-answering\", \"vqa\"`.\n\nThe models that this pipeline can use are models that have been fine-tuned on a visual question answering task. See the up-to-date list of available models on [huggingface.co/models](https://huggingface.co/models?filter=visual-question-answering).\n\n#### \\_\\_call\\_\\_\n\n[](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.VisualQuestionAnsweringPipeline.__call__)[< source \\>](https://github.com/huggingface/transformers/blob/v4.48.1/src/transformers/pipelines/visual_question_answering.py#L79)( image: typing.Union\\[ForwardRef('Image.Image'), str, typing.List\\[ForwardRef('Image.Image')\\], typing.List\\[str\\], ForwardRef('KeyDataset')\\]question: typing.Union\\[str, typing.List\\[str\\]\\] = None\\*\\*kwargs ) ‚Üí A dictionary or a list of dictionaries containing the result. Refer to this class for methods shared across different pipelines.\n\nBase class implementing pipelined operations. Pipeline workflow is defined as a sequence of the following operations:\n\nInput -\\> Tokenization -\\> Model Inference -\\> Post-Processing (task dependent) -\\> Output\n\nPipeline supports running on CPU or GPU through the device argument (see below).\n\nSome pipeline, like for instance [FeatureExtractionPipeline](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/v4.48.1/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.FeatureExtractionPipeline) (`'feature-extraction'`) output large tensor object as nested-lists. In order to avoid dumping such large structure as textual data we provide the `binary_output` constructor argument. If set to `True`, the output will be stored in the pickle format.\n\n#### It should contain at least one tensor, but might have arbitrary other items.\n\n#### push\\_to\\_hub\n\n[](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub)[< source \\>](https://github.com/huggingface/transformers/blob/v4.48.1/src/transformers/utils/hub.py#L828)( repo\\_id: struse\\_temp\\_dir: typing.Optional\\[bool\\] = Nonecommit\\_message: typing.Optional\\[str\\] = Noneprivate: typing.Optional\\[bool\\] = Nonetoken: typing.Union\\[bool, str, NoneType\\] = Nonemax\\_shard\\_size: typing.Union\\[int, str, NoneType\\] = '5GB'create\\_pr: bool = Falsesafe\\_serialization: bool = Truerevision: str = Nonecommit\\_description: str = Nonetags: typing.Optional\\[typing.List\\[str\\]\\] = None\\*\\*deprecated\\_kwargs )\n\nExpand 11 parameters\n\nParameters\n\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.repo_id)**repo\\_id** (`str`) ‚Äî The name of the repository you want to push your pipe to. It should contain your organization name when pushing to a given organization.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.use_temp_dir)**use\\_temp\\_dir** (`bool`, _optional_) ‚Äî Whether or not to use a temporary directory to store the files saved before they are pushed to the Hub. Will default to `True` if there is no directory named like `repo_id`, `False` otherwise.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.commit_message)**commit\\_message** (`str`, _optional_) ‚Äî Message to commit while pushing. Will default to `\"Upload pipe\"`.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.private)**private** (`bool`, _optional_) ‚Äî Whether to make the repo private. If `None` (default), the repo will be public unless the organization‚Äôs default is private. This value is ignored if the repo already exists.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.token)**token** (`bool` or `str`, _optional_) ‚Äî The token to use as HTTP bearer authorization for remote files. If `True`, will use the token generated when running `huggingface-cli login` (stored in `~/.huggingface`). Will default to `True` if `repo_url` is not specified.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.max_shard_size)**max\\_shard\\_size** (`int` or `str`, _optional_, defaults to `\"5GB\"`) ‚Äî Only applicable for models. The maximum size for a checkpoint before being sharded. Checkpoints shard will then be each of size lower than this size. If expressed as a string, needs to be digits followed by a unit (like `\"5MB\"`). We default it to `\"5GB\"` so that users can easily load models on free-tier Google Colab instances without any CPU OOM issues.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.create_pr)**create\\_pr** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) ‚Äî Whether or not to create a PR with the uploaded files or directly commit.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.safe_serialization)**safe\\_serialization** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `True`) ‚Äî Whether or not to convert the model weights in safetensors format for safer serialization.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.revision)**revision** (`str`, _optional_) ‚Äî Branch to push the uploaded files to.\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.commit_description)**commit\\_description** (`str`, _optional_) ‚Äî The description of the commit that will be created\n*   [](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.tags)**tags** (`List[str]`, _optional_) ‚Äî List of tags to push on the Hub.\n\nUpload the pipeline file to the ü§ó Model Hub.\n\n[](https://huggingface.co/docs/transformers/en/main_classes/pipelines#transformers.Pipeline.push_to_hub.example)Examples:\n\nCopied\n\nfrom transformers import pipeline\n\npipe = pipeline(\"google-bert/bert-base-cased\")\n\n\\# Push the pipe to your namespace with the name \"my-finetuned-bert\".\npipe.push\\_to\\_hub(\"my-finetuned-bert\")\n\n\\# Push the pipe to an organization with the name \"my-finetuned-bert\".\npipe.push\\_to\\_hub(\"huggingface/my-finetuned-bert\")\n\n####
